--------------- Extracted Question ---------------

To determine what is to the right of the small yellow circle, let's analyze the information step by step:

1. We have three blocks: A, B, and C.
2. Block B is to the right of block A.
3. Block B contains a small yellow circle and one big blue square.
4. The small yellow circle is below and to the right of the big blue square.

Now, let's consider block C:
5. Block C is to the right of block B.
6. Block C contains a small yellow square.
7. The small yellow square is below and to the left of a big yellow square.
8. The big yellow square is touching the right edge of this block.

Since block C is to the right of block B, and the small yellow circle is in block B, we need to determine what is to the right of the circle in block B.

- In block C, the big yellow square is touching the right edge of the block, and the small yellow square is below and to the left of the big yellow square. Therefore, the big yellow square is positioned further to the right than the small yellow square.

Given this arrangement, the big yellow square, which is touching the right edge of block C, is to the right of the small yellow circle in block B.

Thus, the answer is {1}.

Therefore, neither medium yellow square number two nor the shape that is touching the bottom edge of Block B is directly below the blue square in Block A. The answer is {3}.
Final Answer: 3
